<script>
function pdf() { 
	$ebid.pdf.title = '개찰조서';
	$ebid.pdf.down('개찰조서_교외선 송추~의정부간 재해예방 옹벽설치공사.pdf');
}

// 부적격사유를 조회
function viewUnfitReason(reason) {
	$('#reason').html(reason);
	
	// dialog
	$ebid.dialog.open({
		title: '부적격사유 조회',
		width: '400px'
	});
	
	//v IeProcConformJudgCS get-f20
}

</script>
